    591  34d7							;alreadyBlack2
    592  34d7
    593  34d7							; Handle the player joystick reading. We do it *every frame* so that we can incorporate a two-frame
    594  34d7							; buffer.  This is designed to give a little better responsiveness to the 'quick tap' movement.
    595  34d7
    596  34d7		       a5 90		      lda	BufferedJoystick	; previous frame
    597  34d9		       85 91		      sta	BufferedJoystick+1	; -> buffered
    598  34db
    599  34db
    600  34db							; Create a 'standardised' joystick with D4-D7 having bits CLEAR if the appropriate direction is chosen.
    601  34db							; P2 is shifted UP, so we don't need to worry in usage elsewhere (it's same format as a P1 joystick)
    602  34db
    603  34db		       a5 99		      lda	whichPlayer	; 3
    604  34dd		       25 a7		      and	jtoggle	; 3
    605  34df		       aa		      tax		; 2

    636  3500							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    637  3500							; Player animation happens *every* frame so that we get good animation speeds.  Note that
    638  3500							; the player animation consists of running a small animation 'program', and then actually drawing
    639  3500							; the player.	The draw is the neat bit, because all it does is update some self-modifying pointers
    640  3500							; inside the actual draw kernel in the appropriate bank.
    641  3500
    642  3500
      0  3500					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	AnimatePlayers	; in GENERIC_BANK_1
      1  3500		       00 06	   BANK_AnimatePlayers =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  3500					      SUBROUTINE
      3  3500				   AnimatePlayers
    644  3500
    645  3500							; Optimised 7/1/2012 -- single page tables
    646  3500
    647  3500							; This interesting code performs the animations for the player(s) and sets the
    648  3500							; pointers INSIDE the row bank for the draw code to point to the correct player
    649  3500							; shape.  Kind of neat, as it doesn't require any shape copying (=speed!)
    650  3500
    651  3500
    652  3500							; Cycle the player through his animation list.  The animation of a player is a direct
    653  3500							; pointer to the actual shape used to display the player.  This shape is in turn
    654  3500							; written to the current bank's self-modifying locations for the draw.  Since
    655  3500							; we are effectively drawing from this current bank, the same code can be used
    656  3500							; to 'undraw' the player as required.
    657  3500
    658  3500
    659  3500							; x = player index
    660  3500							; sets ManAnimation = FRAME to display for player
    661  3500							; ManAnimation = index of player program into Manimate list
    662  3500
    663  3500		       24 80		      bit	gameMode
    664  3502		       30 2c		      bmi	AnimationOK	; don't animate during pause
    665  3504
    666  3504		       c6 9f		      dec	ManDelayCount
    667  3506		       10 28		      bpl	AnimationOK
    668  3508
    669  3508		       a4 a0	   ReloadAnimation ldy	ManAnimation
    670  350a		       b9 00 f6    ContinueAnim lda	Manimate,y	; delay count
    671  350d		       d0 07		      bne	NewFrameOK
    672  350f		       b9 01 f6 	      lda	Manimate+1,y
    673  3512		       a8		      tay
    674  3513		       4c 0a f5 	      jmp	ContinueAnim
    675  3516
    676  3516		       10 0d	   NewFrameOK bpl	doDelay
    677  3518
    678  3518		       c8		      iny		; handle a REFLECT
    679  3519		       a5 a3		      lda	ManLastDirection
    680  351b		       29 f7		      and	#%11110111
    681  351d		       19 00 f6 	      ora	Manimate,y
    682  3520		       85 a3		      sta	ManLastDirection
    683  3522
    684  3522		       c8		      iny
    685  3523		       d0 e5		      bne	ContinueAnim
    686  3525
    687  3525		       85 9f	   doDelay    sta	ManDelayCount
    688  3527
    689  3527		       c8		      iny
    690  3528		       b9 00 f6 	      lda	Manimate,y
    691  352b		       85 a2		      sta	ManAnimationFrameLO
    692  352d
    693  352d		       c8		      iny
    694  352e		       84 a0		      sty	ManAnimation
    695  3530
    696  3530		       60	   AnimationOK rts

      0  3535					      include	"i2c_v2.2.inc"
      1  3535							;
      2  3535							; i2c_v2.2.inc
      3  3535							;
      4  3535							;
      5  3535							; AtariVox EEPROM Driver
      6  3535							;
      7  3535							; By Alex Herbert, 2004
      8  3535							;
      9  3535							; Optimisations by Thomas Jentzsch, 2006/2008
     10  3535							;
     11  3535
     12  3535
     13  3535							; I/O Constants
     14  3535
     15  3535		       00 04	   I2C_SDA_MASK equ	$04
     16  3535		       00 08	   I2C_SCL_MASK equ	$08
     17  3535
     18  3535
     19  3535							; Signalling Macros
     20  3535
     21  3535							;  MAC     I2C_SCL_0
     22  3535							;    lda     #$00
     23  3535							;    sta     SWCHA
     24  3535							;  ENDM
     25  3535
     26  3535							;  MAC     I2C_SCL_1
     27  3535							;    lda     #I2C_SCL_MASK
     28  3535							;    sta     SWCHA
     29  3535							;  ENDM
     30  3535
     31  3535							;  MAC     I2C_SDA_IN
     32  3535							;    lda     #I2C_SCL_MASK
     33  3535							;    sta     SWACNT
     34  3535							;  ENDM
     35  3535
     36  3535							;  MAC     I2C_SDA_OUT
     37  3535							;    lda     #I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK
     38  3535							;    sta     SWACNT
     39  3535							;  ENDM
     40  3535
     41  3535
     42  3535					      MAC	i2c_start
     43  3535							; I2C_SCL_1
     44  3535					      lda	#(I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK)*2	; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK
     45  3535					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     46  3535							; I2C_SDA_OUT
     47  3535					      lsr		; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK
     48  3535					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
     49  3535							; total: 12 cycles
     50  3535					      ENDM
     51  3535
     52  3535
     53  3535					      MAC	i2c_txbit
     54  3535							; I2C_SCL_0
     55  3535					      lda	#%0011	; 2
     56  3535					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     57  3535							; set bit
     58  3535					      adc	#%1000	; 2
     59  3535					      sta	SWACNT	; 4	     SDA = !C (a = %1000 / %1100)
     60  3535							; I2C_SCL_1
     61  3535					      lda	#I2C_SCL_MASK	; 2
     62  3535					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     63  3535							; total: 18 cycles
     64  3535					      ENDM
     65  3535
     66  3535
     67  3535					      MAC	i2c_txnack
     68  3535							; I2C_SCL_0
     69  3535					      lda	#I2C_SCL_MASK*2	; 2	     $00
     70  3535					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     71  3535							; I2C_SDA_IN
     72  3535					      lsr		; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK
     73  3535					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
     74  3535							; I2C_SCL_1
     75  3535					      nop		; 2	     required for timing!
     76  3535					      sta	SWCHA	; 4	     I2C_SCL_MASK
     77  3535							; total: 18 cycles
     78  3535					      ENDM
     79  3535
     80  3535
     81  3535							; Subroutine Macros
     82  3535
     83  3535					      MAC	i2c_subs
     84  3535
     85  3535				   i2c_startread
     86  3535							; use V to flag if previous byte needs ACK
     87  3535					      ldy	#%10100001	; 2	     eeprom read command
     88  3535					      .byte	$2c	; 2
     89  3535				   i2c_startwrite
     90  3535					      ldy	#%10100000	; 2	     eeprom write command
     91  3535					      I2C_START		;12	     start signal (clears V flag)
     92  3535					      tya		; 2 = 16
     93  3535				   i2c_txbyte
     94  3535					      eor	#$ff	; 2	     invert data byte
     95  3535					      sec		; 2
     96  3535					      rol		; 2 =	6    shift loop bit into a
     97  3535				   i2c_txbyteloop
     98  3535					      tay		; 2
     99  3535					      I2C_TXBIT		;18	     transmit
    100  3535					      tya		; 2
    101  3535					      asl		; 2	     shift next bit into C
    102  3535					      bne	i2c_txbyteloop	; 2= 26/27
    103  3535
    104  3535							; receive acknowledge bit
    105  3535
    106  3535					      beq	i2c_rxbit	;43 = 43
    107  3535							; i2c_txbyte: 264 cycles
    108  3535							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    109  3535
    110  3535				   i2c_rxbyte
    111  3535					      bvc	i2c_rxskipack	; 2	     previous byte needs acknowledge?
    112  3535					      jsr	i2c_txack	;24	     transmit acknowledge bit
    113  3535
    114  3535				   i2c_rxskipack
    115  3535					      bit	i2c_rxbyte	; 4	     set V - next byte(s) require acknowledge
    116  3535
    117  3535					      lda	#1	; 2
    118  3535				   i2c_rxbyteloop
    119  3535					      tay		; 2 =	2
    120  3535				   i2c_rxbit		;	     receive bit in C
    121  3535					      I2C_TXNACK		;18 = 18
    122  3535
    123  3535					      lda	SWCHA	; 4
    124  3535					      lsr		; 2
    125  3535					      lsr		; 2
    126  3535					      lsr		; 2 = 10    C = SDA
    127  3535
    128  3535					      tya		; 2
    129  3535					      rol		; 2	     rotate into Y
    130  3535					      bcc	i2c_rxbyteloop	; 2=	6/7
    131  3535
    132  3535							; received byte in A
    133  3535					      rts		; 6 =	6
    134  3535							; i2c_rxbit:  40 cycles
    135  3535							; i2c_rxbyte: 310/333 cycles
    136  3535							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    137  3535
    138  3535				   i2c_stopread
    139  3535					      bvc	i2c_stopwrite	; 2
    140  3535					      ldy	#$80	; 2
    141  3535					      jsr	i2c_rxbit	;46	     transmit no-acknowledge
    142  3535
    143  3535				   i2c_stopwrite
    144  3535					      jsr	i2c_txack	;30
    145  3535
    146  3535							; return port to input mode
    147  3535					      lda	#0	; 2	     0
    148  3535					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
    149  3535					      rts		; 6 = 12
    150  3535							; i2c_stopread:  45/92
    151  3535							; i2c_stopwrite: 42
    152  3535							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    153  3535
    154  3535				   i2c_txack
    155  3535							; I2C_SCL_0
    156  3535					      lda	#0	; 2	     $00
    157  3535					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
    158  3535							; I2C_SDA_OUT
    159  3535					      lda	#(I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK)	; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK
    160  3535					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
    161  3535							; I2C_SCL_1
    162  3535					      asl		; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK
    163  3535					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
    164  3535
    165  3535					      rts		; 6
    166  3535							; total: 24 cycles
    167  3535							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    168  3535
    169  3535					      ENDM
    170  3535
    171  3535
    172  3535

    710  35a0
    711  35a0		       06 00	   SAVEKEY_ADR =	$0600	;	     reserved address for Boulder Dash (64 bytes)
    712  35a0
    713  35a0							; SK Memory Map:
    714  35a0							;		 cave	 level
    715  35a0							; $0600-$0602	 A	 1
    716  35a0							; $0603-$0605	 A	 2
    717  35a0							; $0606-$0608	 A	 3
    718  35a0							; $0609-$060b	 A	 4
    719  35a0							; $060c-$060e	 A	 5
    720  35a0							; $060f-$0611	 E	 1
    721  35a0							; $0612-$0614	 E	 2
    722  35a0							; $0615-$0617	 E	 3
    723  35a0							; $0618-$061a	 unused
    724  35a0							; $061b-$061d	 unused
    725  35a0							; $061e-$0620	 I	 1
    726  35a0							; $0621-$0623	 I	 2
    727  35a0							; $0624-$0626	 I	 3
    728  35a0							; $0627-$0629	 unused
    729  35a0							; $062a-$062c	 unused
    730  35a0							; $062d-$062f	 M	 1
    731  35a0							; $0630-$0632	 M	 2
    732  35a0							; $0633-$0635	 M	 3
    733  35a0							; $0636-$063f	 unused
    734  35a0
    735  35a0							;------------------------------------------------------------------------------
      0  35a0					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	ReadSaveKey	; = 2371
      1  35a0		       00 06	   BANK_ReadSaveKey =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  35a0					      SUBROUTINE
      3  35a0				   ReadSaveKey
    737  35a0
    738  35a0							; assume no SaveKey found:
    739  35a0		       a9 ff		      lda	#$ff	; 2	     return $ff if no SaveKey found
    740  35a2		       85 e3		      sta	highScoreSK+2	; 3
    741  35a4
    742  35a4							; setup SaveKey:
    743  35a4		       a5 e4		      lda	startCave	; 3	     load start cave*5 and level
    744  35a6		       a6 b3		      ldx	level	; 3
    745  35a8		       20 e1 f5 	      jsr	SetupSaveKey	;6+853
    746  35ab		       90 52		      bcc	NoSKfound	; 2/3
    747  35ad
    748  35ad							;    lda     #$34
    749  35ad							;    sta     COLUBK
    750  35ad
    751  35ad							; start read
    752  35ad		       20 88 f5 	      jsr	i2c_stopwrite	;6+42	     end of "fake" write
    753  35b0		       20 35 f5 	      jsr	i2c_startread	;6+284      Start signal and $a1 command byte
    754  35b3
    755  35b3							; read high score:
    756  35b3		       a2 02		      ldx	#3-1	; 2 = 1187
    757  35b5				   .loopRead
    758  35b5		       20 5e f5 	      jsr	i2c_rxbyte	;6+333      read byte from EEPROM
    759  35b8		       c9 ff		      cmp	#$ff	; 2	     EEPROM slot empty?
    760  35ba		       d0 02		      bne	.skipEmpty	; 2/3	      no, skip clear
    761  35bc		       a9 00		      lda	#0	; 2	     clear EEPROM slot
    762  35be				   .skipEmpty
    763  35be		       95 e1		      sta	highScoreSK,x	; 4
    764  35c0		       ca		      dex		; 2
    765  35c1		       10 f2		      bpl	.loopRead	; 2/3= 354
    766  35c3
    767  35c3							; stop read:
    768  35c3		       4c 81 f5 	      jmp	i2c_stopread	;3+92=95    terminate read
    769  35c6
    770  35c6							;------------------------------------------------------------------------------
      0  35c6					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	WriteSaveKey	; = 1751
      1  35c6		       00 06	   BANK_WriteSaveKey =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  35c6					      SUBROUTINE
      3  35c6				   WriteSaveKey
    772  35c6
    773  35c6							; check if new high score:
    774  35c6		       a6 e1		      ldx	highScoreSK	; 3
    775  35c8		       e8		      inx		; 2
    776  35c9		       f0 34		      beq	NoSKfound	; 2/3	     no new high score, abort
    777  35cb
    778  35cb							; setup SaveKey:
    779  35cb		       a5 e4		      lda	startCave	; 3	     load start cave*5 and level
    780  35cd		       a6 e5		      ldx	startLevel	; 3
    781  35cf		       20 e1 f5 	      jsr	SetupSaveKey	; 6+853
    782  35d2		       90 2b		      bcc	NoSKfound	; 2/3
    783  35d4
    784  35d4							;    lda     #$64
    785  35d4							;    sta     COLUBK
    786  35d4
    787  35d4							; write high score:
    788  35d4		       a2 02		      ldx	#3-1	; 2 = 841
    789  35d6				   .loopWrite
    790  35d6		       b5 e1		      lda	highScoreSK,x	; 4
    791  35d8		       20 44 f5 	      jsr	i2c_txbyte	;6+264      transmit to EEPROM
    792  35db		       ca		      dex		; 2
    793  35dc		       10 f8		      bpl	.loopWrite	; 2/3= 837
    794  35de
    795  35de							; stop write:
    796  35de		       4c 88 f5 	      jmp	i2c_stopwrite	; 3+42= 45  terminate write and commit to memory
    797  35e1
    798  35e1
    799  35e1							;------------------------------------------------------------------------------
      0  35e1					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	SetupSaveKey	; = 853
      1  35e1		       00 06	   BANK_SetupSaveKey =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  35e1					      SUBROUTINE
      3  35e1				   SetupSaveKey
    801  35e1
    802  35e1							; calculate slot;
    803  35e1							; a = cave (5*n): A=$00; E=$05; I=$0a; M=$0f
    804  35e1							; x = level (0..4)
    805  35e1		       85 e6		      sta	offsetSK	; 3
    806  35e3		       8a		      txa		; 2
    807  35e4		       18		      clc		; 2
    808  35e5		       65 e6		      adc	offsetSK	; 3
    809  35e7		       85 e6		      sta	offsetSK	; 3
    810  35e9		       0a		      asl		; 2	     multiply by 3
    811  35ea		       65 e6		      adc	offsetSK	; 3
    812  35ec		       69 00		      adc	#<SAVEKEY_ADR	; 2
    813  35ee		       aa		      tax		; 2 = 22
    814  35ef							; detect SaveKey:
    815  35ef		       20 38 f5 	      jsr	i2c_startwrite	;6+280
    816  35f2		       d0 0a		      bne	.exitSK	; 2/3
    817  35f4
    818  35f4							; setup address:
    819  35f4		       b8		      clv		; 2
    820  35f5		       a9 06		      lda	#>SAVEKEY_ADR	; 2	     upper byte of address
    821  35f7		       20 44 f5 	      jsr	i2c_txbyte	;6+264
    822  35fa		       8a		      txa		; 2	     x = lower byte offset
    823  35fb		       4c 44 f5 	      jmp	i2c_txbyte	;3+264      returns C==1
    824  35fe
    825  35fe				   .exitSK
    826  35fe		       18		      clc
    827  35ff				   NoSKfound
    828  35ff		       60		      rts
    829  35ff					      ENDIF

     80  3843				   CopyROMShadowToRAM_F000
     81  3843		       a9 f0		      lda	#>$F000
     82  3845
      0  3845					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	CopyROMShadowToRAM	; in INITBANK
      1  3845		       00 07	   BANK_CopyROMShadowToRAM =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  3845					      SUBROUTINE
      3  3845				   CopyROMShadowToRAM
     84  3845
     85  3845							; Function copies a RAM prototype ROM bank into the destination RAM bank.  Typically
     86  3845							; the variable definitions are in the ROM shadow because this allows auto-initialisation
     87  3845							; of the variable contents from ROM declarations, but still allows access to them as
     88  3845							; variables when the correct RAM bank is switched in.	Code is also, of course, copied
     89  3845							; into the RAM destination so that code is callable whenever the ROM *or* RAM bank is
     90  3845							; switched in.  Further, if multiple copies are made to multiple RAM banks, then the
     91  3845							; code co-lives in all banks and may run even as bankswitching occurs between those
     92  3845							; banks -- by the very code itself.
     93  3845
     94  3845							; Note: Relies on ROM_Bank having being set via CALL mechanism to call this function
     95  3845		       85 be		      sta	Board_AddressR+1
     96  3847		       86 df		      stx	O_ROM_Source_Bank	; source bank
     97  3849		       84 c2		      sty	RAM_Bank	; destination bank
     98  384b
     99  384b		       a0 00		      ldy	#0
    100  384d		       84 bd		      sty	Board_AddressR
    101  384f		       84 bf		      sty	Board_AddressW
    102  3851		       a9 14		      lda	#>($1000+RAM_WRITE)
    103  3853		       85 c0		      sta	Board_AddressW+1
    104  3855
    105  3855							; Iterate 4 pages (1K) for complete bank copy
    106  3855
    107  3855		       a9 04		      lda	#4
    108  3857		       85 de		      sta	O_CopyCount
    109  3859
    110  3859		       84 e0	   CopyPage   sty	O_Index
    111  385b		       a5 df		      lda	O_ROM_Source_Bank
    112  385d		       20 3c f8 	      jsr	GetROMByte	; get byte from ROM shadow bank
    113  3860							;tax
    114  3860		       a4 e0		      ldy	O_Index
    115  3862		       a6 c2		      ldx	RAM_Bank
    116  3864		       20 4a f8 	      jsr	PutBoardCharacter	;6+21(A)	 write byte to RAM bank
    117  3867
    118  3867		       a4 e0		      ldy	O_Index
    119  3869		       c8		      iny
    120  386a		       d0 ed		      bne	CopyPage
    121  386c
    122  386c		       e6 be		      inc	Board_AddressR+1
    123  386e		       e6 c0		      inc	Board_AddressW+1
    124  3870
    125  3870		       c6 de		      dec	O_CopyCount
    126  3872		       d0 e5		      bne	CopyPage
    127  3874
    128  3874		       a4 c2		      ldy	RAM_Bank	; TODO: remove!?
    129  3876		       60		      rts
    130  3877

      0  3877					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	SetPlatformColours	; in INITBANK
      1  3877		       00 07	   BANK_SetPlatformColours =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  3877					      SUBROUTINE
      3  3877				   SetPlatformColours
    134  3877
    135  3877							; Now modify the hardwired colours so that we're correctly switched for NTSC/PAL
    136  3877							; The platform (0=NTSC, 1=PAL) is set from the right difficulty switch
    137  3877							; Note: This relies on DrawTheScreen starting on page boundary so that the (),y
    138  3877							; addressing will not violate the page-crossing restriction of 3E.
    139  3877
    140  3877							;		  sty RAM_Bank			  ; we assume we called CopyROMShadowToRAM before
    141  3877
    142  3877		       a9 00		      lda	#<DrawTheScreen	; = 0
    143  3879		       85 bf		      sta	Board_AddressW
    144  387b		       a9 f4		      lda	#>( DrawTheScreen + RAM_WRITE )
    145  387d		       85 c0		      sta	Board_AddressW+1
    146  387f
    147  387f							; first, set the x index (with last one being a RTS ($60))
    148  387f
    149  387f		       a6 c2		      ldx	RAM_Bank
    150  3881		       e0 07		      cpx	#SCREEN_LINES-1	; might become variable when vertical scrolling
    151  3883		       d0 07		      bne	.skipPatch
    152  3885		       a9 60		      lda	#$60	; rts
    153  3887		       a0 41		      ldy	#<SELFMOD_X
    154  3889		       20 4a f8 	      jsr	PutBoardCharacter	;6+21(A)	 set index/rts
    155  388c				   .skipPatch
    156  388c
    157  388c		       a2 02		      ldx	#3-1
    158  388e				   .loopColor
    159  388e		       86 de		      stx	colorIdx
    160  3890							; set PF colors
    161  3890		       b5 ba		      lda	color,x
    162  3892		       bc b7 f0 	      ldy	SelfModColOfsTbl,x
    163  3895							;tax
    164  3895		       a6 c2		      ldx	RAM_Bank
    165  3897		       20 4a f8 	      jsr	PutBoardCharacter	;6+21(A)	 copy PF colour RED/GREEN/BLUE to self-modifying RAM
    166  389a							; set player colors
    167  389a		       a6 de		      ldx	colorIdx
    168  389c		       bd ba f0 	      lda	SelfModePlayerTbl,x
    169  389f		       a4 81		      ldy	Platform
    170  38a1		       c0 02		      cpy	#PAL
    171  38a3		       90 02		      bcc	.platform0
    172  38a5		       69 14		      adc	#LINES_PER_CHAR-1	; C==1!
    173  38a7				   .platform0
    174  38a7		       bc bd f0 	      ldy	SelfModPlayerColOfsTbl,x
    175  38aa							;tax
    176  38aa		       a6 c2		      ldx	RAM_Bank
    177  38ac		       20 4a f8 	      jsr	PutBoardCharacter	;6+21(A)	 copy player colour RED/GREEN/BLUE to self-modifying RAM
    178  38af							; loop
    179  38af		       a6 de		      ldx	colorIdx
    180  38b1		       ca		      dex
    181  38b2		       10 da		      bpl	.loopColor
    182  38b4
    183  38b4		       a4 c2		      ldy	RAM_Bank
    184  38b6		       60		      rts
    185  38b7
    186  38b7				   SelfModColOfsTbl
    187  38b7		       53 86 1c 	      .byte.b	<(SELFMOD_BLUE+1), <(SELFMOD_GREEN+1), <(SELFMOD_RED+1)
    188  38ba				   SelfModePlayerTbl

    192  38c0

      0  78c0					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	SwitchObjects	;=72
      1  78c0		       00 0f	   BANK_SwitchObjects =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  78c0					      SUBROUTINE
      3  78c0				   SwitchObjects
    212  78c0							; TJ: used by:
    213  78c0							; - BANK_FIXED.asm
    214  78c0
    215  78c0							; The game loop has come to an end. The only possible "still happening" thing is the sort, which runs
    216  78c0							; in parallel with other processes (objects, draw stack, etc). We may or may not want to wait for the
    217  78c0							; sort to complete.  This code does all the checks needed to switch to the next game frame.
    218  78c0
    219  78c0		       ad 84 02 	      lda	INTIM	; 4
    220  78c3		       c9 03		      cmp	#SEGTIME_SWITCHOBJECTS	; 2
    221  78c5		       90 f8		      bcc	EarlyAbort	; 2/3= 8
      0  78c7					      STRESS_TIME	SEGTIME_SWITCHOBJECTS
      1  78c7				  -	      IF	TEST_SEGTIME_SWITCHOBJECTS = 1
      2  78c7				  -
      3  78c7				  -
      4  78c7				  -
      5  78c7				  -
      6  78c7				  -
      7  78c7				  -	      echo	"***** WARNING! STRESS_TIME enabled @", ., "! *****"
      8  78c7				  -	      bne	. - 7
      9  78c7					      ENDIF
    223  78c7
    224  78c7							; If we're undertime, then abort. The sort will continue to run, and that's great. Only when
    225  78c7							; we're at the throttle cutoff do we switch game-frames.
    226  78c7
    227  78c7							;sec
    228  78c7		       a5 b5		      lda	Throttle	;3
    229  78c9		       e9 a0		      sbc	#MAX_THROTTLE	;2
    230  78cb		       90 f2		      bcc	EarlyAbort	;2/3		 plenty of time left!
    231  78cd
    232  78cd							; Time is up. But we may be in a level which requires perfect sorting
    233  78cd							; So we check for these levels, and wait for the sort to complete for those.
    234  78cd
    235  78cd		       24 b4		      bit	levelDisplay	;3
    236  78cf		       50 08		      bvc	keepFractional	;2/3		 screen does not require complete sort
    237  78d1
    238  78d1							; We have a level which requires the sort to go to completion
    239  78d1							; Check to see if the sort is finished...
    240  78d1
    241  78d1		       a4 c9		      ldy	sortPtr	;3
    242  78d3		       d0 ea		      bne	EarlyAbort	;2/3		 sort still in progress, so wait
    243  78d5		       a4 c8		      ldy	sortRequired	;3
    244  78d7		       10 e6		      bpl	EarlyAbort	;2/3		 sort still in progress, so wait
    245  78d9
    246  78d9		       85 b5	   keepFractional sta	Throttle	;3		 save fractional 'left over' bit
    247  78db
    248  78db							; Pause the game with B/W switch:
    249  78db
    250  78db		       a5 80		      lda	gameMode
    251  78dd							;		  ora LookingAround		  ; New behavour of looking around pauses creatures when activated.
    252  78dd		       30 14		      bmi	.paused	; pause flag set
    253  78df
    254  78df							; Now that we have completed processing the object stack, we switch
    255  78df							; the stack bank pointers for the next time around.
    256  78df
    257  78df		       a5 85		      lda	ObjStackNum	;3
    258  78e1		       49 01		      eor	#1	;2
    259  78e3		       aa		      tax		;2
    260  78e4		       86 85		      stx	ObjStackNum	;3		 swap stacks @here
    261  78e6
    262  78e6							; STOP the sort so it doesn't corrupt the "other" object stack. Sort may get a look-in immediately after
    263  78e6							; this code is finished, so we don't want it to do something unexpected!
    264  78e6
    265  78e6		       a0 ff		      ldy	#<(-1)	;2
    266  78e8		       84 c8		      sty	sortRequired	;3
    267  78ea		       c8		      iny		;2		 Y==0
    268  78eb		       84 c9		      sty	sortPtr	;3
    269  78ed
    270  78ed							; Initialise the iterator and stack pointer for next time around.
    271  78ed							; Previously the stack pointer auto-initialised by popping the stack. Now we have an iterator it's
    272  78ed							; necessary to initialise both.
    273  78ed
    274  78ed		       84 d1		      sty	ObjIterator	;3		 Y==0
    275  78ef		       94 86		      sty	ObjStackPtr,x	;4
    276  78f1
    277  78f1		       84 89		      sty	ScreenDrawPhase	;3
    278  78f3				   .paused
    279  78f3		       60	   quickExit  rts		;6

      0  7a6b					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	TimeSlice
      1  7a6b		       00 0f	   BANK_TimeSlice =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  7a6b					      SUBROUTINE
      3  7a6b				   TimeSlice
    645  7a6b
    646  7a6b							; FIRST check the time is sufficient for the smallest of the timeslices. Not much point
    647  7a6b							; going ahead if there's insufficient time. This allows the previous character drawing to
    648  7a6b							; be much smaller in time, as they don't have to include the timeslice code overhead.
    649  7a6b
    650  7a6b		       ad 84 02 	      lda	INTIM	; 4
    651  7a6e		       c9 05		      cmp	#SEGTIME_MINIMUM_TIMESLICE	; 2
    652  7a70		       90 da		      bcc	timeExit	; 2(3)
    653  7a72
    654  7a72							; Uses the phase variable to vector to the correct processing code for the given timeslice
    655  7a72							; Code may be in any bank. Avoid the fixed bank at all costs!	Once a section is complete
    656  7a72							; it should increment ScreenDrawPhase.
    657  7a72
    658  7a72							; Switched-in bank(s) are undefined after this function is called!
    659  7a72
    660  7a72		       a9 06		      lda	#BANK_TS_PhaseVectorLO	; 2
    661  7a74		       85 3f		      sta	SET_BANK	; 3
    662  7a76
    663  7a76		       a6 89		      ldx	ScreenDrawPhase	; 3		 current phase of drawing
    664  7a78		       bd 5f f4 	      lda	TS_PhaseVectorLO,x	; 4
    665  7a7b		       85 de		      sta	TS_Vector	; 3
    666  7a7d		       bd 64 f4 	      lda	TS_PhaseVectorHI,x	; 4
    667  7a80		       85 df		      sta	TS_Vector+1	; 3
    668  7a82
    669  7a82		       bd 69 f4 	      lda	TS_PhaseBank,x	; 4
    670  7a85		       85 3f		      sta	SET_BANK	; 3		 switch bank
    671  7a87
    672  7a87		       6c de 00 	      jmp	(TS_Vector)	; 3 = 40	 vector to timeslice handler
    673  7a8a
    674  7a8a							; = 55 minimum return time (if segtime abort)

    677  7a8a

    904  7b73
    905  7b73				   NewFrameBD
    906  7b73							; the (at least) 220 cycles wasted in the above... bugs me!
    907  7b73							; the below is an unrolled version.  I've moved some other code between the sync writes, effectively saving um... 22 cycles/frame.
    908  7b73							; This required TIM64T values to be increased by 1 for each platform (we have actually gained back some usable time :)
    909  7b73

    911  7b75		       10 b3		      bpl	NextCaveLevel	; game-triggered next level

    913  7b79
    914  7b79							; Note: VSYNC must NOT be on when starting a new cave! Else you get annoying TV signals.
    915  7b79

    917  7b7b		       85 42	   .loopVSync sta	WSYNC
    918  7b7d		       85 40		      sta	VSYNC
    919  7b7f		       4a		      lsr
    920  7b80		       d0 f9		      bne	.loopVSync	; branch until VYSNC has been reset
    921  7b82

------- FILE sound/intro1_player.asm LEVEL 3 PASS 3
      0  7b8a					      include	"sound/intro1_player.asm"
      1  7b8a							; TIATracker music player
      2  7b8a							; Copyright 2016 Andre "Kylearan" Wichmann
      3  7b8a							; Website: https://bitbucket.org/kylearan/tiatracker
      4  7b8a							; Email: andre.wichmann@gmx.de
      5  7b8a							;
      6  7b8a							; Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
      7  7b8a							; you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
      8  7b8a							; You may obtain a copy of the License at
      9  7b8a							;
     10  7b8a							;   http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
     11  7b8a							;
     12  7b8a							; Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
     13  7b8a							; distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
     14  7b8a							; WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
     15  7b8a							; See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
     16  7b8a							; limitations under the License.
     17  7b8a
     18  7b8a							; Song author: 
     19  7b8a							; Song name: 
     20  7b8a
     21  7b8a							; @com.wudsn.ide.asm.hardware=ATARI2600
     22  7b8a
     23  7b8a							; =====================================================================
     24  7b8a							; TIATracker Player
     25  7b8a							; =====================================================================
     26  7b8a				   tt_PlayerStart
     27  7b8a
     28  7b8a							; PLANNED PLAYER VARIANTS:
     29  7b8a							; - RAM, speed, player ROM: c0/c1 patterns have same length
     30  7b8a							; - RAM: Pack 2 values (out of cur_pat_index, cur_note_index, envelope_index)
     31  7b8a							;	 into one and use lsr/asl to unpack them, allowing only ranges of
     32  7b8a							;	 16/16 or 32/8 for them, depending on number of patterns, max
     33  7b8a							;	 pattern size and max ADSR size
     34  7b8a							; - ROM: Check if tt_SequenceTable can hold ptrs directly without indexing
     35  7b8a							;	 tt_PatternPtrLo/Hi. Can be smaller if not many patterns get repeated
     36  7b8a							;	 (saves table and decode routine)
     37  7b8a							; - Speed: Inline tt_CalcInsIndex
     38  7b8a							; - Speed: Store ptr to current note in RAM instead of reconstructing it?
     39  7b8a							;	 Might also save the need for cur_note_index
     40  7b8a
     41  7b8a
     42  7b8a							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
     43  7b8a							; Helper macro: Retrieves current note. May advance pattern if needed.
     44  7b8a							; Becomes a subroutine if TT_USE_OVERLAY is used.
     45  7b8a							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
     46  7b8a					      MAC	tt_fetch_current_note
     47  7b8a							; construct ptr to pattern
     48  7b8a				   .constructPatPtr
     49  7b8a					      ldy	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x	; get current pattern (index into tt_SequenceTable)
     50  7b8a					      lda	tt_SequenceTable,y
     51  7b8a					      IF	TT_USE_GOTO = 1
     52  7b8a					      bpl	.noPatternGoto
     53  7b8a					      and	#%01111111	; mask out goto bit to get pattern number
     54  7b8a					      sta	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x	; store goto'ed pattern index
     55  7b8a					      bpl	.constructPatPtr	; unconditional
     56  7b8a				   .noPatternGoto
     57  7b8a					      ENDIF
     58  7b8a					      tay
     59  7b8a					      lda	tt_PatternPtrLo,y
     60  7b8a					      sta	tt_ptr
     61  7b8a					      lda	tt_PatternPtrHi,y
     62  7b8a					      sta	tt_ptr+1
     63  7b8a							; get new note
     64  7b8a					      IF	TT_USE_OVERLAY = 0
     65  7b8a					      ldy	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     66  7b8a					      ELSE
     67  7b8a							; If the V flag is set and if the new note is an instrument,
     68  7b8a							; it means it got pre-fetched by an overlay percussion, it has
     69  7b8a							; to remain in sustain.
     70  7b8a					      clv
     71  7b8a							; check if note had been pre-fetched by overlay perc already
     72  7b8a					      lda	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     73  7b8a					      bpl	.notPrefetched
     74  7b8a							; If so, remove flag
     75  7b8a					      and	#%01111111
     76  7b8a					      sta	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     77  7b8a							; Set V flag for later
     78  7b8a					      bit	tt_Bit6Set
     79  7b8a				   .notPrefetched
     80  7b8a					      tay
     81  7b8a					      ENDIF
     82  7b8a					      lda	(tt_ptr),y
     83  7b8a							; pre-process new note
     84  7b8a							; 7..5: instrument (1..7), 4..0 (0..31): frequency
     85  7b8a							; 0/0: End of pattern
     86  7b8a					      bne	.noEndOfPattern
     87  7b8a							; End of pattern: Advance to next pattern
     88  7b8a					      sta	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x	; a is 0
     89  7b8a					      inc	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x
     90  7b8a					      bne	.constructPatPtr	; unconditional
     91  7b8a				   .noEndOfPattern
     92  7b8a					      ENDM
     93  7b8a
     94  7b8a
     95  7b8a							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
     96  7b8a							; Music player entry. Call once per frame.
     97  7b8a							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
     98  7b8a				   tt_Player  SUBROUTINE
     99  7b8a							; ==================== Sequencer ====================
    100  7b8a							; Decrease speed timer
    101  7b8a		       c6 d3		      dec	tt_timer
    102  7b8c		       10 6e		      bpl	.noNewNote
    103  7b8e
    104  7b8e							; Timer ran out: Do sequencer
    105  7b8e							; Advance to next note
    106  7b8e		       a2 01		      ldx	#1	; 2 channels
    107  7b90				   .advanceLoop
    108  7b90					      IF	TT_USE_OVERLAY = 1
    109  7b90		       20 a6 fb 	      jsr	tt_FetchNote
    110  7b93				  -	      ELSE
    111  7b93				  -	      TT_FETCH_CURRENT_NOTE
    112  7b93					      ENDIF
    113  7b93							; Parse new note from pattern
    114  7b93		       c9 10		      cmp	#TT_INS_PAUSE
    115  7b95					      IF	TT_USE_SLIDE = 0
    116  7b95		       90 55		      bcc	.finishedNewNote
    117  7b97		       d0 3d		      bne	.newNote
    118  7b99				  -	      ELSE
    119  7b99				  -	      beq	.pause
    120  7b99				  -	      bcs	.newNote
    121  7b99				  -
    122  7b99				  -			; --- slide/hold ---
    123  7b99				  -			; Adjust frequency and hold note in sustain.
    124  7b99				  -			; composer/tracker has to make sure that no unwanted
    125  7b99				  -			; under/overflow happens.
    126  7b99				  -			; Note: f = f + (8-(16-x)) = x + f - 8
    127  7b99				  -	      adc	tt_cur_ins_c0,x	; carry is clear after cmp
    128  7b99				  -	      sec
    129  7b99				  -	      sbc	#8
    130  7b99				  -	      sta	tt_cur_ins_c0,x
    131  7b99				  -	      bcs	.finishedNewNote	; unconditional, since legally no underflow can happen (ins>0 or HOLD for ins=0)
    132  7b99					      ENDIF
    133  7b99
    134  7b99							; --- pause ---
    135  7b99				   .pause
    136  7b99							; Get release index for current instrument. Since a pause can
    137  7b99							; only follow an instrument, we don't need to handle percussion
    138  7b99							; or commands.
    139  7b99		       b5 da		      lda	tt_cur_ins_c0,x
    140  7b9b		       20 34 fc 	      jsr	tt_CalcInsIndex
    141  7b9e		       b9 69 fe 	      lda	tt_InsReleaseIndexes-1,y	; -1 b/c instruments start at #1
    142  7ba1							; Put it into release. Skip junk byte so index no longer indicates
    143  7ba1							; sustain phase.
    144  7ba1		       18		      clc
    145  7ba2		       69 01		      adc	#1
    146  7ba4		       90 44		      bcc	.storeADIndex	; unconditional
    147  7ba6
    148  7ba6							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    149  7ba6							; Helper subroutine to minimize ROM footprint. Will be inlined if
    150  7ba6							; TT_USE_OVERLAY is not used.
    151  7ba6							; Interleaved here so player can be inlined.
    152  7ba6							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    153  7ba6					      IF	TT_USE_OVERLAY = 1
    154  7ba6				   tt_FetchNote
      0  7ba6					      TT_FETCH_CURRENT_NOTE
      1  7ba6
      2  7ba6				   .constructPatPtr
      3  7ba6		       b4 d4		      ldy	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x
      4  7ba8		       b9 7c ff 	      lda	tt_SequenceTable,y
      5  7bab					      IF	TT_USE_GOTO = 1
      6  7bab		       10 06		      bpl	.noPatternGoto
      7  7bad		       29 7f		      and	#%01111111
      8  7baf		       95 d4		      sta	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x
      9  7bb1		       10 f3		      bpl	.constructPatPtr
     10  7bb3				   .noPatternGoto
     11  7bb3					      ENDIF
     12  7bb3		       a8		      tay
     13  7bb4		       b9 72 ff 	      lda	tt_PatternPtrLo,y
     14  7bb7		       85 dc		      sta	tt_ptr
     15  7bb9		       b9 77 ff 	      lda	tt_PatternPtrHi,y
     16  7bbc		       85 dd		      sta	tt_ptr+1
     17  7bbe
     18  7bbe				  -	      IF	TT_USE_OVERLAY = 0
     19  7bbe				  -	      ldy	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     20  7bbe					      ELSE
     21  7bbe
     22  7bbe
     23  7bbe
     24  7bbe		       b8		      clv
     25  7bbf
     26  7bbf		       b5 d6		      lda	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     27  7bc1		       10 07		      bpl	.notPrefetched
     28  7bc3
     29  7bc3		       29 7f		      and	#%01111111
     30  7bc5		       95 d6		      sta	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     31  7bc7
     32  7bc7		       2c 3a fc 	      bit	tt_Bit6Set
     33  7bca				   .notPrefetched
     34  7bca		       a8		      tay
     35  7bcb					      ENDIF
     36  7bcb		       b1 dc		      lda	(tt_ptr),y
     37  7bcd
     38  7bcd
     39  7bcd
     40  7bcd		       d0 06		      bne	.noEndOfPattern
     41  7bcf
     42  7bcf		       95 d6		      sta	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     43  7bd1		       f6 d4		      inc	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x

    156  7bd5		       60		      rts
    157  7bd6					      ENDIF
    158  7bd6
    159  7bd6
    160  7bd6							; --- start instrument or percussion ---
    161  7bd6				   .newNote

    200  7bf1				  -	      ldy	tt_SequenceTable,x	; Current pattern index now in y

    203  7bf1				  -	      sta	tt_timer

    205  7bf1				  -			; Test for odd/even frame
    206  7bf1				  -	      lda	tt_cur_note_index_c0
    207  7bf1				  -	      lsr
    208  7bf1				  -	      lda	tt_PatternSpeeds,y	; does not affect carry flag

    210  7bf1				  -	      and	#$0f	; does not affect carry flag

    214  7bf1				  -	      lsr

     15  7e5b							; See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
     16  7e5b							; limitations under the License.
     17  7e5b
     18  7e5b							; Song author: 
     19  7e5b							; Song name: 
     20  7e5b
     21  7e5b							; @com.wudsn.ide.asm.hardware=ATARI2600
     22  7e5b
     23  7e5b							; =====================================================================
     24  7e5b							; TIATracker melodic and percussion instruments, patterns and sequencer
     25  7e5b							; data.
     26  7e5b							; =====================================================================
     27  7e5b				   tt_TrackDataStart
     28  7e5b
     29  7e5b							; =====================================================================
     30  7e5b							; Melodic instrument definitions (up to 7). tt_envelope_index_c0/1 hold
     31  7e5b							; the index values into these tables for the current instruments played
     32  7e5b							; in channel 0 and 1.
     33  7e5b							; 
     34  7e5b							; Each instrument is defined by:
     35  7e5b							; - tt_InsCtrlTable: the AUDC value
     36  7e5b							; - tt_InsADIndexes: the index of the start of the ADSR envelope as
     37  7e5b							;	 defined in tt_InsFreqVolTable
     38  7e5b							; - tt_InsSustainIndexes: the index of the start of the Sustain phase
     39  7e5b							;	 of the envelope
     40  7e5b							; - tt_InsReleaseIndexes: the index of the start of the Release phase
     41  7e5b							; - tt_InsFreqVolTable: The AUDF frequency and AUDV volume values of
     42  7e5b							;	 the envelope
     43  7e5b							; =====================================================================
     44  7e5b
     45  7e5b							; Instrument master CTRL values
     46  7e5b				   tt_InsCtrlTable
     47  7e5b		       07 04 0c 04*	      dc.b	$07, $04, $0c, $04, $0c
     48  7e60
     49  7e60
     50  7e60							; Instrument Attack/Decay start indexes into ADSR tables.
     51  7e60				   tt_InsADIndexes
     52  7e60		       00 0e 0e 1e*	      dc.b	$00, $0e, $0e, $1e, $1e
     53  7e65
     54  7e65
     55  7e65							; Instrument Sustain start indexes into ADSR tables
     56  7e65				   tt_InsSustainIndexes
     57  7e65		       08 19 19 2b*	      dc.b	$08, $19, $19, $2b, $2b
     58  7e6a
     59  7e6a
     60  7e6a							; Instrument Release start indexes into ADSR tables
     61  7e6a							; Caution: Values are stored with an implicit -1 modifier! To get the
     62  7e6a							; real index, add 1.
     63  7e6a				   tt_InsReleaseIndexes
     64  7e6a		       09 1b 1b 2c*	      dc.b	$09, $1b, $1b, $2c, $2c
     65  7e6f
     66  7e6f
     67  7e6f							; AUDVx and AUDFx ADSR envelope values.
     68  7e6f							; Each byte encodes the frequency and volume:
     69  7e6f							; - Bits 7..4: Freqency modifier for the current note ([-8..7]),
     70  7e6f							;	 8 means no change. Bit 7 is the sign bit.
     71  7e6f							; - Bits 3..0: Volume
     72  7e6f							; Between sustain and release is one byte that is not used and
     73  7e6f							; can be any value.
     74  7e6f							; The end of the release phase is encoded by a 0.
     75  7e6f				   tt_InsFreqVolTable
     76  7e6f							; 0: Pizzicato bassb
     77  7e6f		       8a 8a 89 88*	      dc.b	$8a, $8a, $89, $88, $86, $85, $85, $84
     78  7e77		       83 00 83 83*	      dc.b	$83, $00, $83, $83, $83, $00
     79  7e7d							; 1+2: Square2
     80  7e7d		       8c 8c 8b 89*	      dc.b	$8c, $8c, $8b, $89, $87, $85, $84, $83
     81  7e85		       82 82 81 81*	      dc.b	$82, $82, $81, $81, $81, $00, $81, $00
     82  7e8d							; 3+4: Square
     83  7e8d		       85 85 85 85*	      dc.b	$85, $85, $85, $85, $84, $83, $83, $82
     84  7e95		       82 82 81 81*	      dc.b	$82, $82, $81, $81, $81, $81, $00, $80
     85  7e9d		       00		      dc.b	$00
     86  7e9e
     87  7e9e
     88  7e9e
     89  7e9e							; =====================================================================
     90  7e9e							; Percussion instrument definitions (up to 15)
     91  7e9e							;
     92  7e9e							; Each percussion instrument is defined by:
     93  7e9e							; - tt_PercIndexes: The index of the first percussion frame as defined
     94  7e9e							;	 in tt_PercFreqTable and tt_PercCtrlVolTable
     95  7e9e							; - tt_PercFreqTable: The AUDF frequency value
     96  7e9e							; - tt_PercCtrlVolTable: The AUDV volume and AUDC values
     97  7e9e							; =====================================================================
     98  7e9e
     99  7e9e							; Indexes into percussion definitions signifying the first frame for
    100  7e9e							; each percussion in tt_PercFreqTable.
    101  7e9e							; Caution: Values are stored with an implicit +1 modifier! To get the
    102  7e9e							; real index, subtract 1.
    103  7e9e				   tt_PercIndexes
    104  7e9e		       01 0a 0c 	      dc.b	$01, $0a, $0c
    105  7ea1
    106  7ea1
    107  7ea1							; The AUDF frequency values for the percussion instruments.
    108  7ea1							; If the second to last value is negative (>=128), it means it's an
    109  7ea1							; "overlay" percussion, i.e. the player fetches the next instrument note
    110  7ea1							; immediately and starts it in the sustain phase next frame. (Needs
    111  7ea1							; TT_USE_OVERLAY)
    112  7ea1				   tt_PercFreqTable
    113  7ea1							; 0: Kick
    114  7ea1		       00 01 02 03*	      dc.b	$00, $01, $02, $03, $04, $05, $06, $87
    115  7ea9		       00		      dc.b	$00
    116  7eaa							; 1: HH
    117  7eaa		       80 00		      dc.b	$80, $00
    118  7eac							; 2: Snare
    119  7eac		       01 03 06 0e*	      dc.b	$01, $03, $06, $0e, $13, $11, $15, $14
    120  7eb4		       17 1b 00 	      dc.b	$17, $1b, $00
    121  7eb7
    122  7eb7
    123  7eb7							; The AUDCx and AUDVx volume values for the percussion instruments.
    124  7eb7							; - Bits 7..4: AUDC value
    125  7eb7							; - Bits 3..0: AUDV value
    126  7eb7							; 0 means end of percussion data.
    127  7eb7				   tt_PercCtrlVolTable
    128  7eb7							; 0: Kick
    129  7eb7		       ee ed ed eb*	      dc.b	$ee, $ed, $ed, $eb, $e9, $e8, $e8, $e6
    130  7ebf		       00		      dc.b	$00
    131  7ec0							; 1: HH
    132  7ec0		       87 00		      dc.b	$87, $00
    133  7ec2							; 2: Snare
    134  7ec2		       8b 8a 8a 8a*	      dc.b	$8b, $8a, $8a, $8a, $8a, $8a, $89, $88
    135  7eca		       87 86 00 	      dc.b	$87, $86, $00
    136  7ecd
    137  7ecd
    138  7ecd
    139  7ecd							; =====================================================================
    140  7ecd							; Track definition
    141  7ecd							; The track is defined by:
    142  7ecd							; - tt_PatternX (X=0, 1, ...): Pattern definitions
    143  7ecd							; - tt_PatternPtrLo/Hi: Pointers to the tt_PatternX tables, serving
    144  7ecd							;	 as index values
    145  7ecd							; - tt_SequenceTable: The order in which the patterns should be played,
    146  7ecd							;	 i.e. indexes into tt_PatternPtrLo/Hi. Contains the sequences
    147  7ecd							;	 for all channels and sub-tracks. The variables
    148  7ecd							;	 tt_cur_pat_index_c0/1 hold an index into tt_SequenceTable for
    149  7ecd							;	 each channel.
    150  7ecd							;
    151  7ecd							; So tt_SequenceTable holds indexes into tt_PatternPtrLo/Hi, which
    152  7ecd							; in turn point to pattern definitions (tt_PatternX) in which the notes
    153  7ecd							; to play are specified.
    154  7ecd							; =====================================================================
    155  7ecd
    156  7ecd							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    157  7ecd							; Pattern definitions, one table per pattern. tt_cur_note_index_c0/1
    158  7ecd							; hold the index values into these tables for the current pattern
    159  7ecd							; played in channel 0 and 1.
    160  7ecd							;
    161  7ecd							; A pattern is a sequence of notes (one byte per note) ending with a 0.
    162  7ecd							; A note can be either:
    163  7ecd							; - Pause: Put melodic instrument into release. Must only follow a
    164  7ecd							;	 melodic instrument.
    165  7ecd							; - Hold: Continue to play last note (or silence). Default "empty" note.
    166  7ecd							; - Slide (needs TT_USE_SLIDE): Adjust frequency of last melodic note
    167  7ecd							;	 by -7..+7 and keep playing it
    168  7ecd							; - Play new note with melodic instrument
    169  7ecd							; - Play new note with percussion instrument
    170  7ecd							; - End of pattern
    171  7ecd							;
    172  7ecd							; A note is defined by:
    173  7ecd							; - Bits 7..5: 1-7 means play melodic instrument 1-7 with a new note
    174  7ecd							;	 and frequency in bits 4..0. If bits 7..5 are 0, bits 4..0 are
    175  7ecd							;	 defined as:
    176  7ecd							;	 - 0: End of pattern
    177  7ecd							;	 - [1..15]: Slide -7..+7 (needs TT_USE_SLIDE)
    178  7ecd							;	 - 8: Hold
    179  7ecd							;	 - 16: Pause
    180  7ecd							;	 - [17..31]: Play percussion instrument 1..15
    181  7ecd							;
    182  7ecd							; The tracker must ensure that a pause only follows a melodic
    183  7ecd							; instrument or a hold/slide.
    184  7ecd							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    185  7ecd		       00 1f	   TT_FREQ_MASK =	%00011111
    186  7ecd		       00 08	   TT_INS_HOLD =	8
    187  7ecd		       00 10	   TT_INS_PAUSE =	16
    188  7ecd		       00 11	   TT_FIRST_PERC =	17
    189  7ecd
    190  7ecd							; Intro left
    191  7ecd				   tt_pattern0
    192  7ecd		       11 08 3e 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $3e, $08, $12, $3e, $3e, $08
    193  7ed5		       13 08 3e 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $3e, $08, $12, $3e, $3e, $08
    194  7edd		       11 08 3e 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $3e, $08, $12, $3e, $12, $3e
    195  7ee5		       13 08 3e 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $3e, $08, $12, $3e, $13, $08
    196  7eed		       00		      dc.b	$00
    197  7eee
    198  7eee							; Intro2 L
    199  7eee				   tt_pattern1
    200  7eee		       11 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $34, $08
    201  7ef6		       13 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $34, $08
    202  7efe		       11 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $12, $34
    203  7f06		       13 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $13, $08
    204  7f0e		       00		      dc.b	$00
    205  7f0f
    206  7f0f							; Intro2-fill L
    207  7f0f				   tt_pattern2
    208  7f0f		       11 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $34, $08
    209  7f17		       13 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $34, $08
    210  7f1f		       11 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $12, $34
    211  7f27		       13 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $13, $08
    212  7f2f		       00		      dc.b	$00
    213  7f30
    214  7f30							; Intro right
    215  7f30				   tt_pattern3
    216  7f30		       6f 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$6f, $08, $73, $08, $6e, $08, $73, $08
    217  7f38		       6f 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$6f, $08, $73, $08, $73, $08, $73, $08
    218  7f40		       6f 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$6f, $08, $73, $08, $6e, $08, $b3, $08
    219  7f48		       6f 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$6f, $08, $73, $08, $b3, $08, $73, $08
    220  7f50		       00		      dc.b	$00
    221  7f51
    222  7f51							; Intro2 R
    223  7f51				   tt_pattern4
    224  7f51		       71 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$71, $08, $73, $08, $74, $08, $71, $08
    225  7f59		       6f 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$6f, $08, $73, $08, $b3, $08, $73, $08
    226  7f61		       b3 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$b3, $08, $73, $08, $b3, $08, $73, $08
    227  7f69		       71 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$71, $08, $73, $08, $74, $08, $71, $08
    228  7f71		       00		      dc.b	$00
    229  7f72
    230  7f72
    231  7f72
    232  7f72
    233  7f72							; Individual pattern speeds (needs TT_GLOBAL_SPEED = 0).
    234  7f72							; Each byte encodes the speed of one pattern in the order
    235  7f72							; of the tt_PatternPtr tables below.
    236  7f72							; If TT_USE_FUNKTEMPO is 1, then the low nibble encodes
    237  7f72							; the even speed and the high nibble the odd speed.
    238  7f72				  -	      IF	TT_GLOBAL_SPEED = 0
    239  7f72				  -tt_PatternSpeeds
    240  7f72				  -%%PATTERNSPEEDS%%
    241  7f72					      ENDIF
    242  7f72
    243  7f72
    244  7f72							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    245  7f72							; Pattern pointers look-up table.
    246  7f72							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    247  7f72				   tt_PatternPtrLo
    248  7f72		       cd ee 0f 30	      dc.b	<tt_pattern0, <tt_pattern1, <tt_pattern2, <tt_pattern3
    249  7f76		       51		      dc.b	<tt_pattern4
    250  7f77				   tt_PatternPtrHi
    251  7f77		       fe fe ff ff	      dc.b	>tt_pattern0, >tt_pattern1, >tt_pattern2, >tt_pattern3
    252  7f7b		       ff		      dc.b	>tt_pattern4
    253  7f7c
    254  7f7c
    255  7f7c							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    256  7f7c							; Pattern sequence table. Each byte is an index into the
    257  7f7c							; tt_PatternPtrLo/Hi tables where the pointers to the pattern
    258  7f7c							; definitions can be found. When a pattern has been played completely,
    259  7f7c							; the next byte from this table is used to get the address of the next
    260  7f7c							; pattern to play. tt_cur_pat_index_c0/1 hold the current index values
    261  7f7c							; into this table for channels 0 and 1.
    262  7f7c							; If TT_USE_GOTO is used, a value >=128 denotes a goto to the pattern
    263  7f7c							; number encoded in bits 6..0 (i.e. value AND %01111111).
    264  7f7c							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    265  7f7c				   tt_SequenceTable
    266  7f7c							; ---------- Channel 0 ----------
    267  7f7c		       00 00 01 02*	      dc.b	$00, $00, $01, $02, $80
    268  7f81
    269  7f81
    270  7f81							; ---------- Channel 1 ----------
    271  7f81		       03 04 03 04*	      dc.b	$03, $04, $03, $04, $85
    272  7f86
    273  7f86
 Track size:  $12b
    274  7f86					      echo	"Track size: ", *-tt_TrackDataStart

   1129  7f86					      ECHO	"FREE BYTES IN FIXED BANK = ", $FFFB - *
   1130  7f86

   1132  7f86							; The reset vectors
   1133  7f86							; these must live in the fixed bank (last 2K of any ROM image in TigerVision)
   1134  7f86
   1135  8000 ????				      SEG	InterruptVectors
   1136  7ffc					      ORG	FIXED_BANK + $7FC
   1137  7ffc					      RORG	$7ffC
   1138  7ffc
   1139  7ffc							;		 .word Reset	       ; NMI	    (not used)
   1140  7ffc		       ec fa		      .word.w	Reset	; RESET
   1141  7ffe		       ec fa		      .word.w	Reset	; IRQ	      (not used)
   1142  8000
   1143  8000							;---------------------------------------------------------------------------
